Conversation/Tutorial/Line00032,许多异虫生物可以在战场上从进行形态变异，从而变得更加强大。异虫建筑也有同样的功能，它们可以通过变异来获得生产新单位的能力。 /// Many Zerg creatures can morph from one form to another on the battlefield. Zerg structures can also mutate from one form to another, growing more powerful and unlocking new unit types as they do.=1033

Conversation/Tutorial/Line00034,菌毯是一种有机生长物，会从基地向外延伸。大多数的异虫单位在菌毯上可以移动的更快，除了孵化场，所有的异虫建筑都必须放置在菌毯上。离开菌毯的建筑会慢慢死亡。 /// Creep is an organic growth that spreads around any Zerg base. Most Zerg units will move more quickly when they're on creep, and all Zerg structures except Hatcheries must be built on it. Structures that are no longer on creep will slowly die.=1035
Conversation/Tutorial/Line00035,孵化场、虫后和王虫都可以分泌菌毯，你可以借助这些单位或建筑来延伸菌毯的面积。 /// Creep is generated by Hatcheries, Queens, and Overlords, so you can use these units and structures to expand your creep.   =1036
